Important Foreign Telegrams

Meeting of the General Commission of the Disarmament Conference

Leading Principles Still Not Agreed Upon

Amendments to the Step-by-Step Reduction Plan

Few Responded to China's Proposal

Guomin News Agency, Geneva, 18th - After the General Commission of the Disarmament Conference met today, the representatives began talking about the issue of holding another conference in a few years in just a few minutes. As for the leading principles of this conference, no agreement was reached at today's meeting. Although several representatives spoke, they only delivered grand eloquence, strongly arguing that it is necessary to convene several conferences to gradually reduce armaments.

Stimson Missed the Meeting Due to a Cold

Today's General Commission was convened at 10:17 AM. When the representatives entered the venue one after another, a tense atmosphere was already evident in the venue. Representatives and attendees were eagerly awaiting the arrival of U.S. Secretary of State Stimson. Chairman Henderson waited near the door, but only Gibson was seen arriving after more than ten minutes, so he returned to the chairman's seat. Mr. Gibson reported that Stimson was unable to attend due to a cold, and the meeting officially began.

Put Forward the Basic Principles of the German-Turkish Proposal

Chairman Henderson asked the representatives to express their opinions on the principles for guiding the conference, hoping to obtain a feasible basis for global disarmament. He also put forward the principles proposed by the German and Turkish representatives, advocating that the conference should adopt a simple and grand convention to completely solve the disarmament problem, claiming that if this principle is rejected by the assembly, then the conference will follow the principle of gradual reduction to carry out the work. German representative Nadolny spoke first, proposing that compulsory disarmament should be the guiding principle of the conference, claiming that if there is sincerity and faithful willingness to seek disarmament, then what Germany has done, other countries should follow. He then tried his best to describe the propriety of the German-Turkish proposal, persuading the representatives to abandon selfish national policies, take genuine disarmament as the only aspiration, and jointly promote the progress of the conference, declaring that if we today only reaffirm the existing disarmament foundation and have no other achievements, we will violate the purpose and spirit of the League of Nations charter. German Chancellor Brüning also did not attend the meeting, so Mr. Nadolny spoke.

Joint Proposal of Six Small Countries

Next was the joint proposal of the representatives of Belgium, Czechoslovakia, Norway, Nicaragua, Denmark, and Estonia, advocating gradual reduction of armaments, believing that the implementation of Article 8 of the charter is the only way, stating that disarmament can only be carried out in stages, with continuous amendments in the shortest possible time. Then France put in great effort to support this proposal, and Poland also strongly defended it. The German representative then requested that this resolution be amended.

Litvinov's Speech Contained Irony

Soviet People's Commissar for Foreign Affairs Litvinov also took the stage to speak, ridiculing the representatives who advocated a gradual disarmament plan, saying with a smile that this conference should not first achieve success in the path of disarmament as a starting point for efforts, and then transfer most of the work to the second and third conferences.

Then British Foreign Secretary Simon spoke, expressing agreement with the idea of reopening the conference and making constant amendments, but said that this conference must have some real achievements, claiming that we should not spend this long day in Geneva year after year.

China Proposes Complete Disarmament

Next, the Chinese representative took the stage and put forward a plan for complete disarmament, which was more radical and grand than anything contributed by any other representative, shocking the audience. The Chinese representative advocated that the conference should determine the armaments that each country should have, giving serious consideration to the truly important elements of a country's national defense and stipulating the minimum limit required for its appropriate defense, claiming that a country's armaments should be based on the size of the national territory, the number of people, the length and nature of the border, and the domestic resources, and the convenience of its land, sea, and air transportation, and the degree of security against foreign aggression should also be considered. This Chinese proposal took into account both moral and material aspects, not only advocating the abolition of certain armaments, but also wanting to create a practical plan to promote spiritual disarmament throughout the world, saying that the current governments of the world have failed to seek disarmament from the psychological and moral aspects, and therefore there are still those who support narrow nationalism and try their best to cultivate the warlike spirit of the people. As for the material aspect, they advocated abolishing all aggressive weapons such as battleships, submarines, aircraft carriers, heavy artillery, all military aircraft, and all chemical and bacteriological warfare.

The Step-by-Step Reduction Plan Dominates

However, many in the meeting agreed to gradually reduce armaments, and few responded to the radical proposals of China and Germany. Japan, Switzerland, France, Poland, Sweden, England, Italy, Persia, and the Netherlands successively took the stage and all agreed to the joint proposal of the six small countries. Germany, Turkey, and the Soviet Union all requested that this joint proposal be amended before it was put to a vote. Chairman Henderson then transferred the proposal to the drafting committee to revise the text and adjourned the meeting at 12:30 PM.

Japanese Stocks Plunge

Telecommunication Agency, Tokyo, 18th - The Japanese financial world is expecting the Bank of Japan to cut interest rates, but Japan's domestic and foreign financial situation is deteriorating day by day. The stock market was dominated by sellers again today. The Tokyo stock market initially showed low prices, and in the afternoon, cotton yarn, raw silk, and major stocks continued to fall sharply. The recent sharp drop in the shares of Tokyo New Stocks was the most severe, reaching a low of 138 yen. Compared with the peak of buying after the gold embargo, which was 179.9 yen at the end of November, it has fallen by nearly 40 yen.

Stimson Meets with Brüning

Thorough Discussion of Disarmament and Other Issues

Anglo-American Views on Foreign Policy Are Close

Guomin News Agency, Geneva, 17th - U.S. Secretary of State Stimson had a long talk with German Chancellor Brüning and Undersecretary of State Pürlo this evening. Polish Finance Minister Goes to France

Domestic Industries on the Verge of Bankruptcy

Will Borrow Huge Sums from France

Guomin News Agency, Warsaw, 18th - Polish Finance Minister Grün suddenly went to Paris today, likely related to the plan to borrow huge sums from France again, so the financial world is paying great attention. It is said that Poland will be unable to maintain itself without borrowing, because although the country is an agricultural country, it can resist economic decline for a little longer than a purely industrial country, but domestic industries are on the verge of bankruptcy. The major industries are feeling especially poor because the National Bank recently refused to discount Soviet bonds. For example, some factories in Upper Silesia only have enough cash to cover a few days of expenses. It is now expected that France may take the opportunity to propose harsher conditions, but Poland will face a serious crisis without prompt assistance.

Match King Forged Italian Treasury Bills

Formally Confirmed by Italian Authorities

France Suffers Huge Losses

Guomin News Agency, Rome, 17th - Today, local authorities formally confirmed that forged Italian treasury bills with a face value of 21 million pounds were found in the assets of the Kreuger Company. It is said that the counterfeit bills bear the forged signature of former Italian Finance Minister Boselli, but it is extremely clumsy. Those who regularly trade international bonds cannot be deceived. Furthermore, Italy and Match King Kreuger have never had any financial relationship. Around 1930, Kreuger contacted the Italian government to provide huge loans in order to obtain a match monopoly, but the Italian government immediately rejected it.

Guomin News Agency, Amsterdam, 17th - The chief financial columnist for Telegraph newspaper today discussed the recent developments of the Kreuger & Toll Company and estimated that French people purchased more than 500 million francs worth of shares in the company and its subsidiaries. Therefore, after Sweden, France may suffer the heaviest losses.

Scheduled Opening of Lithuania Case

Hague, 17th (National Dispatch) - Today, the office of the President of the International Court of Justice announced that the case of the four signatory countries of the Memel Convention against the Lithuanian government will be publicly tried on June 22nd. The plaintiffs in this case are the governments of Britain, France, Italy, and Japan, accusing Lithuania of violating the Memel Convention by using coercive measures to force the Memel Parliament to organize an administrative committee. The Parliament refused, and was subsequently dissolved.

Geneva, 17th (Havas) - The International Trade Union Congress, which studied the problems of economic panic and unemployment, has concluded. Great Flood in Yugoslavia Causes Disaster

Belgrade, 18th (National Dispatch) - A great flood in southern Yugoslavia has caused a disaster, with thousands of houses submerged and residents homeless. The authorities have come up with a surprising plan to use bomber planes to drop bombs and destroy dikes, hoping to spread the flood more widely in order to reduce the water's force. However, some farmers do not agree with this measure and have fired at the planes, although there have been no reports of damage to the aircraft.

New Zealand Sailors Prepare to Strike

Auckland, 18th (Reuters) - It is rumored today that sailors may announce a strike immediately. Although the city is quiet at the end of the week, troublemakers are still lurking everywhere, so people are still very panicked. Zeppelin Airship Flies to South America

Friedrichshafen, 17th (National Dispatch) - The second flight of the Graf Zeppelin airship, delayed by two days, started its third flight today and has resumed its original schedule. It departed from here at 0:05 this morning, bound for Pernambuco, Brazil, and is expected to arrive the day after tomorrow, and return on the 22nd, arriving back here on the 25th. After one more flight, the tropical rainy season will begin, and the flights will be temporarily suspended, to resume in the autumn.

Important News

League of Nations and Japan Heading for Direct Conflict

Britain and the United States Take the Same Stance on the Puppet State

The U.S. Will Close its Embassy in Tokyo

Osaka Mainichi Shimbun, Geneva - The Committee of Nineteen has already met, and the future of the Sino-Japanese problem is expected to undergo major developments. The central point of the issue is that, formally, Article 15 of the Covenant will be applied to deal with the Manchurian Incident. However, it is difficult to predict what attitude the League of Nations will actually take. However, Secretary-General Drummond has already stated to Representative Sato that the Manchurian problem must be dealt with under Article 15 of the Covenant. Furthermore, with U.S. Secretary of State Stimson actively involved in Geneva and the Chinese representative flying the flag of the Nine-Power Treaty, the Manchurian problem will undoubtedly turn into a major drama. Although Stimson has not made a clear statement, his attitude is expected to shift with the situation. Therefore, fundamental problems are likely to arise in Manchuria. In particular, Japan's direct conflict with the League of Nations over the application of Article 15 is becoming increasingly urgent. On the other hand, what is most noteworthy is that when the United States adopts a tough stance towards Japan, Britain will also follow suit and adopt the same approach. In this way, Britain and the United States are bound to stand on a common front against Japan. Moreover, U.S. Deputy Foreign Minister Ito Taisho answered questions in the Lower House, and decided not to recognize Manchuria as an independent country, so the gloomy future of Manchuria is already expected.

Osaka Mainichi Shimbun, Washington - U.S. Secretary of State Stimson has submitted a budget reduction proposal to the Senate, intending to close embassies and consulates abroad. Although he has not yet specified which countries or locations will be affected, it is reported that the embassy in Tokyo is also among those to be closed.

Japanese to Add Consulates in Northeast China

And Add Police Stations Along the South Manchuria Railway

Dalian Correspondence - In order to realize its concrete plan to invade Northeast China, the Japanese are now preparing to establish consulates in Dunhua, Ningguta, Tao'an, and Hailun, and consular branches in Fuyu, Yimianpo, Mao'ershan, (Linjiang) Sanxing, Muling, and five other locations. In addition, they will also add eleven police stations along the South Manchuria Railway. All consulates, branches, and police stations are scheduled to be established one after another in mid-month. The annual budget is estimated at ten million, which Foreign Minister Yoshizawa has obtained the understanding of various cabinet members. This funding will be formally added to the budget plan.

Investigation Team Reports Situation from Nanjing (8)

Appendix: The League of Nations' Handling of the Sino-Japanese Dispute

The Chairman's declaration stated that, in order to maintain world peace and promote the resolution of the Sino-Japanese dispute, the Executive Yuan unanimously resolved to send personnel to Manchuria for on-site investigation. The content of this resolution is explained in detail in sections: The first section of the resolution reaffirms the validity of the resolution unanimously passed by the Executive Yuan on September 30, insisting that Japanese troops should withdraw to within the South Manchuria Railway line within the shortest possible period under the conditions stipulated in that article. The Executive Yuan attaches great importance to this resolution and hopes that both governments can earnestly implement it. The second section expresses deep regret that the situation that occurred after the previous adjournment of the Executive Yuan was even more serious and caused legitimate concern to all parties. Therefore, both parties should immediately restrain themselves and avoid the recurrence of warfare and any actions that would expand the dispute. The fourth section requests that the governments of other countries report to the League of Nations at any time on the situation reported by their representatives in Manchuria, as past experience has proven that such information is of great use. Countries that currently have such representatives stationed in Manchuria should maintain the status quo and strive to increase their effectiveness. The governments of the aforementioned countries should also continue to engage with the Chinese and Japanese governments so that the Chinese and Japanese governments can at any time request their local representatives to work in a certain location. The fifth section states that the investigation team to be dispatched is of a consultative nature and has extremely broad powers. In principle, the team's powers extend to all matters that hinder international relations and Sino-Japanese peace, or upon which Sino-Japanese peace depends, and they may all be studied. The governments of China and Japan may also request the investigation team to study all issues. The team may also freely select all issues as materials for reporting to the Executive Yuan. When necessary, it may report special circumstances to the Executive Yuan at any time. When the investigation team arrives at its destination, if the two parties have not yet implemented the resolution of September 30, the team should report the situation to the Executive Yuan. If the two parties are directly involved in issues related to military affairs, the team cannot interfere, but the team can of course act freely in collecting information for reporting purposes. The meaning of the explanation of the fifth section in the Chairman's declaration, which was not clearly stated in the resolution, is that (1) the provision that the two governments may request the team to study all issues is to satisfy Japan's investigation of our country's anti-Japanese boycott movement and demands, because the Japanese representative requested that this meaning be included in the resolution, which was opposed by our country's representative; (2) the provision that when the team arrives at its destination, if the two parties have not yet implemented the resolution of September 30, the team should immediately report the situation to the Executive Yuan is because our country gave up the demand for a deadline for troop withdrawal and intended to indirectly stipulate a deadline for troop withdrawal in the resolution, which was opposed by the Japanese representative, so it was included in the Chairman's declaration.

In practice, this resolution only reiterates the validity of the September 30 resolution. However, from September 30 to December 10, more than two months have passed. During this period, Qiqihar and many railways have been occupied by Japanese troops. The result of this meeting is only to send an investigation team. Although the effectiveness of this team is difficult to predict at present, the fact has proven that it is a delaying tactic for Japan. The team's work cannot be completed in less than six months. During this time, Japan's various facilities in the Eastern Provinces can be completed, and the great powers will be helpless.

C. Attitudes of Various Countries

(1) Great Powers After Japan detained the Eastern Provinces' salt tax, which had nothing to do with the lives and property of Japanese residents, and captured Qiqihar, the governments of Britain, France, the United States, and other countries knew that Japan's so-called self-defense was just a pretext, and the spirit of the League of Nations Covenant had been completely destroyed. If China and Japan were small European countries, the League of Nations would have issued an order to attack long ago, and Japan would have withdrawn its troops automatically before the order was even issued. However, Japan is a powerful country in the Far East, and the victim is China, a country on the verge of internal strife and political collapse. Therefore, the great powers believe that if they force Japan, a madman, to abide by the law, it will harm themselves. China is a prodigal son, and is it worth sacrificing for? It's better to just wait and see. This was the attitude of the great powers at the time.

However, since Japan violated the Executive Yuan's resolution of September 30, the so-called reputation of the empire, which has always valued morality, has been completely lost, and its hideous face has been exposed to the world. Therefore, Japan's only hope lies in a final struggle. Unless the great powers intervene militarily or our country recognizes its annexation of Manchuria, there is no other way to stop its barbaric actions. Speaking of the issue of military intervention, on the surface, it seems that the Executive Yuan of the League of Nations can pass a resolution based on Articles 15 and 16 of the Covenant, and then order its 50 member countries to cooperate with the United States to take military action against Japan. However, in reality, it is a very complex and difficult problem to solve if the great powers are to make significant sacrifices for this, because the United States has not yet joined the League of Nations. Therefore, if something happens in the Far East, Britain will bear the brunt. Moreover, at that time, the League of Nations was still discussing the Sino-Japanese dispute within the scope of Article 11. According to the provisions of the League of Nations Covenant, all resolutions must be approved by both parties. In legal terms, the resolution of September 30 did not stipulate a deadline for troop withdrawal, and the draft resolution of October 24 was not recognized by Japan, so Japan had no obligation to implement it. Therefore, the British and French governments believed that it was fortunate that peace had been maintained, and hoped that when the investigation team's work was completed, China and Japan could reach a reasonable compromise so that Japanese troops could eventually withdraw. In this way, the League of Nations could barely maintain its image, and the great powers could avoid making sacrifices.

Since Britain and the United States had this plan, the other countries, such as France and Italy, were happy to follow. As a result, although Japan's tyranny was even worse than at the previous meeting, the great powers had reached the point where they could not advance any further except by using force to maintain the Covenant. Therefore, their attitude changed from being cowardly to being fearful.

(2) Small Countries As for the small and weak countries, because their position is different from that of the great powers, and the only obstacle to the integrity of their own territory lies in the League of Nations and the Kellogg-Briand Pact, they all hope that the great powers can thoroughly resolve the current Sino-Japanese dispute. However, because they themselves have no real power and only hope for the sacrifices of the great powers, they find it difficult to speak out. Therefore, except for the eloquent Spanish representative, the other representatives are all silent. This is regrettable. (The End)

Jiangxi Bandits Invade Southern Fujian Again

One Group Takes the Route of Ruijin into Tingzhou

Fujian Troops Are Jointly Suppressing Them with Guangdong Troops

Fuzhou Correspondence - After the Jiangxi bandits were jointly suppressed by the Guangdong troops under Yu Hanmou, they fled from Ganzhou to the Yudu Ningdu area, and also sent another group to take the route of Ruijin into the Fujian Province's Tingzhou Ninghua to obtain food. As for the Guangdong troops under Huang Renhuan, they have been concentrating in various places in Guangdong Province, such as Dabu and Jiaoling, and can attack Wuhang within a few days, and then attack Changting from Wuhang to reach Ruijin, with the aim of attacking Yudu in conjunction with the First Army troops entering Jiangxi. According to the reports of Yang Fengnian, the brigade commander of Zhang Zhen's division, Yongding, Longyan, and Liancheng counties are currently peaceful. (April 9)

Phenomena in Jingdezhen, Jiangxi

The Shanghai War Has a Very Pessimistic Impact on the Porcelain Industry's Future

All Factories Have Not Resumed Work Due to Troop Transfers

Nanchang Correspondence - Jingdezhen is located in the northeastern part of Jiangxi Province, bordering southern Anhui to the north and western Zhejiang to the east. Geographically speaking, it is actually the屏藩(bastion/barrier) of Jiangxi, Zhejiang, and Anhui. Since the Song Dynasty, it has been famous for its porcelain production. For more than a thousand years, it has been known as a porcelain industrial area, with more than 200,000 workers. It was attacked and captured by bandits three times in the past two years, resulting in tens of millions in losses to industry and commerce, reaching a state of bankruptcy. In recent years, the 55th Division has been stationed there, and the bandit atmosphere has been slightly suppressed, and the market has gradually recovered. However, with the outbreak of the Shanghai War, financial stagnation has greatly affected the town's porcelain industry. In addition to a small number of porcelain merchants in Tianjin, Hong Kong, and other places, most others have hesitated to come. As a result, the town's industry and commerce have been virtually suspended, and the city's economic difficulties have reached an extreme point. The sources of funds for education, industry, and other expenses have all fallen through. Last month, the industrial and commercial circles, in view of this, held a meeting to discuss relief measures, intending to quickly urge the factories to resume work, and at the same time, the Chamber of Commerce would borrow money from the banking community in Shanghai to tide over the workers' lives. According to the town's custom, all factories start work on the first day of the third month of the lunar calendar. All workers who come to the town to work, regardless of whether work has started or not, will have their food costs borne by the employers from the first day of the third month of the lunar calendar. Therefore, many workers only bring travel expenses. This year, in the midst of efforts to provide relief, the 55th Division suddenly received orders to return to Anhui. The people of the town feared that the bandits would take advantage of the vacancy and return, and were all extremely panicked. As a result, the factories did not dare to resume work, and the entire town was plunged into a state of panic. The industrial and commercial circles specially appointed Lai Qing and Shi Wenmo as representatives to petition the central and Jiangxi provincial high-level authorities, requesting that the 55th Division not be transferred until the replacement troops had been designated, in order to maintain security, so that the town's 200,000 workers would not lose their jobs and be incited by the Red Bandits.

Wuhu's Relief Efforts for Disaster Victims

All Circles Organize Financial Maintenance Association

Wuhu Correspondence - The County Water Conservancy Engineering Committee is currently facing the fact that more than 100,000 disaster victims in the four rural areas are without clothing or food, and urgently needs to seek relief. It was previously planned to collect deeds worth one million, which would be transferred to the rice merchants through the Chamber of Commerce to borrow 50,000 piculs of rice for the disaster-stricken farmers, to be repaid with principal and interest after the autumn harvest. However, due to the importance of the matter, it was decided to convene a joint meeting of party, government, military, police, gentry, and business circles at the county government on the 17th of this month to discuss the measures. If this measure is implemented, the disaster victims in the entire county can maintain their food supply for 100 days.

Since the Wuhu city suffered a flood last year, followed by the outbreak of the Shanghai War, the financial situation has been extremely difficult, and most businesses are on the verge of bankruptcy. In order to provide financial relief and maintain the market, the Wuhu County Chamber of Commerce convened a joint meeting of all circles on the 13th, and decided to organize a Financial Maintenance Association. It was stipulated that the committee would consist of 15 members, two recommended by the banking community, one from the money shops, seven from various industries, and one each from the party, government, military, and police. Chen Houer and Hu Dongchen were appointed to draft the organizational outline, and it was decided to hold a second meeting of all circles on the 16th to present and implement it.

The Xiehe Company's Shenglong small steamer, which runs between Datong and Wuhu, departed from Datong to Wuhu on the morning of the 13th. When it arrived near Daxin Island, it was suddenly surrounded and robbed by more than 30 bandits, resulting in a total loss of about 10,000 yuan in cash, gold bars, and drafts.

Quotation First Increases, Then Decreases

Active Trading, Chinese Merchants Mostly Buy, Few Sell

Various merchant groups did not need much, but except for a few solid businesses on the customer side who were able to continue, even those who had settled their payments from the previous period would probably have difficulty, not to mention ordinary businesses. As for long-term deposits, large amounts of funds coming in and out were still tied to interbank transfers, so they were transferred at similar rates.

Cotton Yarn and Cotton Sales Were Quiet

The cotton yarn market remained dull with no improvement. This was because the sales of existing yarn were slow, the situation was uncertain, which dampened sentiment. The foreign interest rate was still difficult to recover. The farmers are busy in the mainland, and there is no hope for yarn sales. The Yangtze River has been suspended for a long time, so the bottom goods have increased. The statistics of each bank's purchases throughout the day were 300 packages, and the market price fell slightly by 0.025 qian. Customer banks in the north purchased 30 packages, 60 packages were purchased in the mainland, 20 packages were purchased in Anqing, 35 packages were purchased in Guangdong, 10 packages were purchased in Changsha, 7 packages were purchased by Hankou banks, and 40 packages were purchased in Shantou, and 60 packages were purchased by other banks.

Decline in Consumption of Sock Factories, Sharp Decline in Fine Yarn

The fine yarn market has recently declined sharply, with a significant downward trend. In previous years, there was usually a period of growth during the spring sales season, as white cloth was most popular in the summer. For example, in the Jiangsu and Zhejiang areas, sock factories were numerous and demand was considerable. However, since the Japanese invasion this year, the war has made financial circulation impossible and sales have been severely affected. The price of 42-count "Ren Zhong" yarn in March reached 342 taels, but now it sells for 296 taels, a drop of 46 taels. The price of 32-count "Ren Zhong" yarn was 256 taels, but now it is 232 taels, a drop of 24 taels. This kind of decline is sharp, and the future is not optimistic. After the sudden change in the political situation in the Northeast last year, the supply of the thread was insufficient and sock factories were facing the risk of suspending operations. Later, they used British thread to supplement. The crisis was resolved, but the price was as high as over 400 taels. Recalling the situation of the previous rise and the current fall, one cannot help but feel the difference between then and now.

Sparse Purchases of Raw Cotton by Factories

The cotton market is calm, and the foreign cotton situation is showing signs of softening, but the exchange rate is still weak, so sentiment is flat. The factories' attitude is very calm, and they have little intention of purchasing. This is because yarn sales are not smooth. According to some, after the outbreak of the Shanghai war, the Japanese factories were completely closed. They purchased a lot of American and Indian cotton last year, and now they have a surplus due to lack of demand and want to sell it off. Now, Indian merchants are selling 1,000 bales of Indian cotton to the Shenxin Factory, priced at 30.5 taels, with spot goods delivered to the factory. However, the inventory of domestic cotton is exhausted, and the sources of supply from all regions are depleted. Only Shenxin Factory still has some purchases, with 1,000 bales of Xingheng cotton opened, priced at 30 and a half taels. The spot goods were sent to the factory.

According to the current situation, the carryover for this season will increase by 30% compared to last year. The futures market still followed the US cotton market. As a result, there was still hope for an increase. Spot sales were flat, and prices did not fluctuate much. Transactions were speculative in nature. Fewer Buyers, Price of Rice Flour Declines

Recently, as the 20th approached, those without the strength only gave up. Sales were also sluggish because the market was rising step by step, and customer banks inevitably waited and watched. Therefore, when the opening price was offered, the initial price of the April navy ship was 2.1225 taels, and the May price was 2.1475 taels. Very Few Silkworms Reared in Lanxi

Only Two or Three Tenths of Previous Years... The Early Batch Has Just Begun to Collect Ants

The silkworm season in Lanxi, Jinhua, Zhejiang is earlier than in Hangzhou and Shaoxing. This year, farmers have learned from the failure of last year's silkworm rearing, and are also facing economic hardship, with no way to borrow money for silkworm rearing. They are generally hesitant and only families with mulberry trees are breeding improved varieties in reduced quantities. Very few people are rearing silkworms, and the amount is only two or three tenths of previous years. The Grain Rain solar term is approaching, and the early batch of silkworms has just begun to collect ants.

Foreign Silk Market is Increasingly Sluggish

Yesterday, the foreign silk market in this port was increasingly sluggish. Foreign firms in Europe and the United States, seeing the sharp decline in overseas silk prices, and Chinese silk merchants, because of the cost of silk, insisted on not selling at a loss, all adopted a wait-and-see attitude, and the market atmosphere was calm. Yesterday, Jardine Matheson only imported ten packages of Sichuan yellow filature, and Xiangli imported twelve packages of yellow coarse silk, and the prices remained flat.

Free Discussion

Record of Platoon Leader Wang, Bao Zheng

Wang's given name is forgotten. During the Zhili-Fengtian War, he served as a platoon leader. Later, when the troops disintegrated, he resigned and returned home to concentrate on business. He was good at management and had accumulated a lot of wealth. When the Shanghai War broke out, the volunteer army rose up and was at its peak. Ambitious people rushed to join. Wang cried out, "Now is the time to repay the country and avenge our hatred!" He packed his bags and went to see General Cai Tingkai of the 19th Route Army and asked to be enlisted. General Cai saw that he was tall and burly and spoke eloquently, so he questioned him on various key military matters. Wang answered fluently and without any errors. He was assigned to the rear team for reserve duty. Wang insisted on rushing to the front line, even shedding tears. General Cai could not bear to disobey his wishes and agreed. At that time, the two sides were in a truce. Wang quietly lay in the trenches, waiting for the enemy to approach, and then fired his gun. His bullets never missed, and he killed countless enemies. When the authorities heard of this, they promoted him to platoon leader. Not long after, the order to charge was given. Wang raised his knife and pointed at the enemy, bravely leading the charge. Wherever the spear tip reached, the enemy scattered. The prestige of our army was greatly enhanced. General Cai praised his bravery and promoted him to company commander and transferred him to the rear for rest. Wang went forward and said, "The old hatred has been avenged, and my wish has been fulfilled. Why should I be greedy for fame and fortune?" He removed his uniform and weapons and left without looking back. Later, according to his companions, Wang's father was killed by the Japanese in Qingdao, and this trip was purely for revenge.

Traitor, Gong Yu

After the Battle of Shanghai, a new term suddenly emerged, namely, the Jiangbei traitor. Newspapers printed daily articles on Jiangbei traitors being hired by the Japanese to throw grenades in various places in the concession. As our army retreated, there were more and more traitors, all referred to as Jiangbei. As a result, people from all walks of life despised those from Jiangbei. In fact, those who willingly acted as traitors were not limited to Jiangbei. Some of the traitors captured in the early stages of the war were not from Jiangbei. Newspaper reports can be cited. For example, in Wusong recently, there is also a puppet organization, and the people in it are not from Jiangbei. However, society did not investigate and mistakenly believed that all traitors were necessarily from Jiangbei. As a result, all Jiangbei people were on the list of those who were despised. Furthermore, from ideological contempt, it progressed to factual exclusion, resulting in Jiangbei people after the war being unable to stand in Shanghai. For example, those who hired servants or rickshaw pullers refused Jiangbei people. Even refugee shelters did not accept Jiangbei refugees. This is truly unjust. Jiangbei is not a place name, but a general term for the area north of the Yangtze River. The people of the counties north of the Yangtze River already have differences in good and bad, civilized and uncivilized. And Jiangbei people living in Shanghai are not entirely unpatriotic. Today, Jiangbei people are refused a foothold in Shanghai, so the laborers who are unwilling to be traitors cannot live and cannot return to their hometowns. They will be forced to go to Zhabei to become traitors. Therefore, in the future, we hope that writers will carefully examine the origin of traitors and not use the term Jiangbei indiscriminately, so that justice can be served.

World News in Brief

The World's First Aviator: The aviation industry today can be considered a golden age. However, very few people know who the world's first aviator was. This person was a Brazilian from South America named Bartolomeu De Gusmao. He passed away more than a hundred years ago. For more than a hundred years, almost no one mentioned him. Today, Brazilians remember their origins and the pioneer who started the trend of aviation. They plan to build a monument to him to inspire. According to Brazilian research, he first flew as early as 1705. Whether this is true is still questionable. Brazilians and Portuguese have drawings depicting his strange aircraft that he originally flew. But he did fly once in 1709. There is a letter written by the Queen of Portugal to her mother the day after the flight as proof. She said, "I saw Gusmao's aircraft rise rapidly and happily into the air." He flew twice in total. The first time he flew as high as a three-story building and circled the building before safely landing. The second time, however, he did not fly successfully. He went up and then fell. (Hai Ke)

The Shanghai War and Military Weapons (XIII) - Yi Zang

Gunpowder and Explosives: The origin of gunpowder is very ancient. China already had it during the Han Dynasty. Its use for launching is said to have started with the Arabs and then spread to Europe. But the Arabs' gunpowder was black, a mixture of saltpeter, sulfur, and charcoal, which is exactly the same as the composition of pine resin, saltpeter powder, and charcoal used by the Chinese. Japanese gunpowder was transmitted from China. In the mid-seventeenth century, the Germans invented a brown gunpowder. In 1845, they invented a wire gunpowder. European countries used it to equip guns and cannons. In 1884, the French invented smokeless cotton gunpowder. China's major ordnance factories can also manufacture it. As for the highly explosive yellow gunpowder, it was created by the French Di Erban. In recent years, countries have used it to equip field guns or as grenades. In the mid-nineteenth century, a tea-brown gunpowder was invented in Europe. However, the gunpowder used in military affairs today can be divided into three types: launching gunpowder,

destructive gunpowder, and blasting gunpowder. In terms of composition, it can be divided into chemical gunpowder and mixed gunpowder. Smokeless gunpowder is beneficial for launching and is loaded into rifles, machine guns, and small- and medium-caliber cannons. Mixed gunpowder is mostly used in cannons. However, there are many types of smokeless gunpowder. Its use varies depending on the type of gun and cannon and the nature of the gunpowder. In general, the main explosive for shells is yellow medicine, tea-brown medicine, or tea-yellow medicine. The main components of various explosives are mostly nitrates, chlorates, and perchlorates. Recently, due to scientific progress and the development of manufacturing technology, the quality of gunpowder has gradually improved. There are solvent-free gunpowder, flame-extinguishing gunpowder, high-speed gunpowder, and non-hygroscopic gunpowder in launching gunpowder. Therefore, the power of guns and cannons has become more and more fierce.

A Heroic Death (Part 2) - Mo Yi

Half an hour later, the enemy was not as reckless as before, and rushed over, dodged and flashed behind more than thirty tank vehicles. Obviously, after receiving their first lesson, they didn't dare act recklessly anymore, so they used the newest type of war machine – the tank vehicle – as their talisman to charge.

Our brave soldiers proposed to the leader:

"If we want to kill all those short devils, we have to get rid of those bastard vehicles!"

And so, a team of daredevils with the responsibility of destroying the enemy's tank vehicles, immediately formed. There were a total of forty brave warriors. Every one of them was covered in petrol and full of explosives.

As the tank vehicles rushed within very close range of the trenches, the forty warriors who were fighting for the glory of the Chinese people, then rushed out; every tank vehicle was like a venomous dragon, spitting bullets that would kill people. Our brave soldiers threw their grenades up; just as if tossing chicken eggs onto stone, only seeing the grenades exploding, and the tank vehicles still impudently charging over, and as if with a contemptuous smile saying, "No matter how fierce you guys are, this time you probably can't do anything to us!"

The forty warriors, just like forty starving tigers, spreading their arms, their heads lowered, hurried and split up to seize their objective. After they had gotten very close to the tank vehicles, then they all fell to the ground, as if struck by bullets. The enemies driving the tank vehicles, all smiling, showed off how powerful, how sturdy their war machines were, thinking that this time there definitely wouldn't be any obstacles in their advance. They didn't know, when those several tank vehicles climbed over the forty warriors' bodies, that the bulky vehicle bodies, were pressing down on the explosives with natures like wildfire, in an instant causing those newest type of war machines of the twentieth century to lose their power of movement, only hearing the sounds of explosion reverberating underneath the wide vehicle treads; the vehicles were severely shaken, and just like a majestic animal, bearing severe wounds, convulsing; the echoes of the explosion, seemed to be sending out mocking noises of triumph. The executioners on top of the tank vehicles, also dumbstruck and didn't know what to do; at the same time amidst the shouts of triumph from our rushing up warriors, they all became our prisoners and spoils of war.

"Old Zhao, you died so tragically. Alas, even your bones aren't here."

But you died with satisfaction. The enemies on top of the tank vehicles, we will definitely kill every one of them, to avenge you; you can rest easy. … Old Zhao, we'll see you again in twenty years! …

Old Zhang, at the time he and the enemies were fighting in close quarters, while he was killing the enemies, in his mouth, he was comforting the old Zhao who had died underneath the tank vehicles… (End)

Shen Bao This Port Supplement

Talk

What is "Normal State"?

— Jin

According to news from the Kuomin News Agency yesterday, Mr. Hymans, Chairman of the Nineteen-Nation Committee of the League of Nations, is currently consulting with both Chinese and Japanese representatives. One of the most important points is the interpretation of the "normal state." Isn't this a ridiculous and pointless matter? If we're talking about reasons why a normal state cannot be restored, I have a few points to make. If the desire is to restore a normal state, this ridiculous and joking question, no matter if we ask Western logicians, legal scholars, or Chinese annotators like Zheng Kangcheng and Yan Shigu to interpret it, no one will have the ability to explain this ridiculous term properly.

First, how can a normal state be restored under the pressure of the Japanese army's heavy forces? The reason why a normal state cannot be restored is entirely due to the Japanese forces stationed in large numbers. Therefore, to restore a normal state, the Japanese army must first completely withdraw.

Second, who should be the subject for determining whether a normal state has been restored? Should we use our country's observation as the standard? Should we use the Japanese observation as the standard? Or should we use a third party's observation as the standard? Suppose other countries believe that a normal state has been restored, but the Japanese say no and do not believe that a normal state has been restored, then what will happen?

Third, even if China and Japan largely agree that a normal state has been restored, but the Japanese have many tricks, either using plainclothes teams or taking advantage of Chinese traitors to stir up trouble from within, then how can a normal state be restored?

Fourth, since our country experienced this war, the losses to commerce and the people cannot be counted with numbers. Even if the war ends here, the purchasing power of the people has already decreased significantly. Not only is there no ability to buy Japanese goods, but there is also no ability to buy goods from other countries. How can a normal state be restored? Moreover, where the army arrives, houses become ruins, spring planting is missed, and how can there be a harvest in autumn? Soldiers and bandits are everywhere, and the people have nowhere to die. How can a normal state be restored?

Therefore, for the League of Nations committee to consider the four characters "normal state" as important and to want to interpret them is truly the biggest joke in the world. Now, the members of the League of Nations only need to recognize the two points resolved by the League of Nations General Assembly:

One, the League of Nations does not recognize or tolerate the destruction of China's territorial integrity and political sovereignty.

Two, resolving the current dispute under the force of arms and other coercion is illegal. If the League of Nations members can recognize these two points, then this pointless and ridiculous question need not be considered any further.

Mass Literature and Art

Spring Rain

— Zhu Zun

Spring sorrow resembles spring bamboo shoots, sprouting in clusters with rain,

Spring rain is like spring tears, dripping all night until dawn.

Spring rain will sometimes end, but my tears never stop,

Dropping onto the grass below the steps, the grass doesn't turn green.

Sprinkling on the fish in the pond, the fish in the pond suddenly don't live.

I ask you, why are you alone? Is there some great injustice?

Why not ride a tall steed, alongside those heading to important posts,

While beauties with faces like flowers, leisurely stroll in Luoyang City.

What are the spring clouds saying? They say they are the souls of war ghosts,

Ascending to heaven and descending to earth, turning into rain pouring down.

What is the purpose of the pouring rain? To wash your brain clean,

Wash your brain clean, do not be blinded by fame and fortune.

Ghosts have no day to return to being human, a lost nation is hard to recover.

Not using the critical points to reinforce the desperate position,

Instead, handing over the map to the enemy.

Oh, the limitless hatred of monkeys, cranes, and insects turning to dust!

Dilapidated walls and broken wells see a temporary renewal.

More than a month of hard fighting with all gains abandoned;

Hearing of the troop movement, tears wet my scarf.

Mass Science

Semi-Automatic Rifle

— Zuo Yi (Translation)

Recently, someone in the United States invented a new type of rifle called the semi-automatic rifle (Scmiautomatic Rfile). The American military authorities are currently testing it. Once the test is passed, all previously used rifles will be discarded and replaced with this new type of rifle.

For decades, many people have been engaged in designing semi-automatic rifles, but the results have not been satisfactory. Recently, more than a dozen types have been submitted to the US government for testing. Currently, only two types are being tested, one made by J. D. Pedersen and the other made by J. C. Garand.

Regarding the advantages of semi-automatic rifles, U.S. Army officer Hatcber reported to the American Society of Mechanical Engineers, mainly as follows:

"The current army rifle in use is the so-called repeating rifle. The repeating rifle has a magazine containing five cartridges. After one cartridge is fired, the mechanism is manually operated to eject the empty cartridge and load a new cartridge for continuous firing. However, operating the mechanism is complicated and requires great force, which often delays the opportunity or causes the aim to be lost. The semi-automatic rifle is different. All cartridge replacement actions are mostly handled by the cartridge itself, and the user only needs to press a button, which is extremely effortless. Therefore, once aimed, continuous firing is possible without missing the target due to cartridge replacement. In future wars, aircraft will be very active, and troops are at risk of being attacked at any time. If a repeating rifle is used, the mechanism must be manually operated each time a shot is fired. For rapidly moving objects such as aircraft, it is difficult to aim and shoot continuously. Therefore, the semi-automatic rifle is preferred."

The application of automatic ammunition firing to machine guns has been around for many years, but the bulkiness of machine guns is not a problem, while rifles must be as light as possible. It is not easy to install an automatic mechanism on a rifle without increasing its weight. The difficulty of success of the semi-automatic rifle lies in this. There are already several types of semi-automatic hunting rifles, but their firepower is very different from that of military rifles. In the future, the US military will inevitably switch to this type of semi-automatic rifle, which is beyond doubt. The great powers' attention to armaments is evident. What are the thoughts of the Chinese people on this?

East, West, South, North

The Feelings of a Newspaper Vendor

— Wu

Ah Bao, a fourteen-year-old newspaper vendor, started calling out on the streets when the sounds of cannons shook the tiles and the fire lit up the sky. At that time, his business was very good, so that scene was particularly deeply etched in his memory. For example, at that time, as long as he shouted loudly, "Want to see the Eastern □□ suffer defeat?" someone would smile lightly at him and scold him softly, "Little rascal," and then happily buy a copy… He thought his business skills were indeed not bad, even much better than those opium smokers. But once, on a very bustling street, he saw a female newspaper vendor, who looked like a female student of eighteen or nineteen years old, whose sales skills were excellent. She didn't even need to shout; as long as she walked along, many people would naturally rush to her with smiles, even making her so busy that her hands and feet were in a fluster. However, he himself couldn't get any business at the same time and in the same place, so he had to run away dejectedly. He thought:

"Damn it, I just don't believe that newspapers sold by women smell better?"

However, now it's even more different. Business is simply non-existent. Even if he runs to the entrance of the big mansions that he rarely goes to and shouts until his throat is sore, no one is seen to generously buy a copy. What is the reason for this? He thought it was because he wasn't shouting "Eastern □□ are suffering defeat", right? But his father had already told him that he couldn't shout that anymore and could only simply call out "Want the newly published…" What can be done about this?

But now the market is indeed very different: for example, the signs posted on the store doors used to say "…boycott to resist humiliation," but now it says "endure the pain and open the market"; before, there was crying and weeping everywhere from people moving, but now there are rickshaws carrying beautiful girls wearing brand new spring clothes; before, there was the rumbling of cannons, but now there is the "Western laugh" of the phonograph. Everything is "the earth returning to spring," everything is the peaceful scene of "Greater Shanghai," a "free city." So, the movie theaters are filled with light-hearted laughter, so this little newspaper vendor is no longer noticed, and even that eighteen- or nineteen-year-old female newspaper vendor is no longer in fashion, right?

In short, now the Easterners have won, and everyone doesn't need to read the newspaper anymore, so why don't they just stop fighting? This is a big loss for the little newspaper vendor's family!

Odds and Ends

Also a Jiangbei Person

— Zhisheng

Yesterday afternoon, I was chatting with some friends about current affairs, talking eloquently and with great interest. Just as we were about to drink tea to quench our thirst, we suddenly heard a water chestnut seller singing in front of the door. So we called him in, chose the fruit, and discussed the price. The price was not right, and one of my classmates jokingly said to him, "Your heart is too black. Why don't you serve the Japanese? Then your income would be much more than from this peddling."

This person glared and scolded, "You gentlemen are all knowledgeable and polite, so why would you utter such evil words to slander me? Those who are traitors are not all my fellow Jiangbei people. People from other places also sometimes do it, but Jiangbei people account for the majority. However, the name of disloyalty has been entirely placed on Jiangbei people. Although I am foolish and lowly, I have known since I was young that loving the country is important. Therefore, during this incident, some people may have invited me to join the traitors, but I always refused. I sincerely know that being a traitor must be profitable, but when the cunning rabbit dies, the hunting dog is cooked. What benefit is there in profit? Therefore, I am willing to engage in this lowly occupation, enduring hardship and living in peace."

When I heard this, I stood up in awe and concluded the deal regardless of the price. Afterwards, I thought, a Jiangbei person like this truly does not lose his integrity as a Jiangbei person. The good and bad among people are inherently uneven. We cannot condemn everyone because of the bad behavior of one person. Therefore, Confucius said, "In a village of ten households, there must be someone of loyalty and integrity," which is exactly what he meant. For example, even between the brothers of Liu Xiahui and Zhi (Dao Zhi), there are differences between the good and the bad. Although some Jiangbei people are willing to be traitors, there may also be some who devote themselves to serving the country. Therefore, I quickly recount this to show that not all Jiangbei people are traitorous.

There are indeed many Jiangbei people who are traitors. Therefore, in the local news or in the articles submitted by gentlemen, they often scold Jiangbei people. I also deeply hate Jiangbei people and deeply feel sorry for them, because I clearly know that Jiangbei people are not completely traitors. Now, I have received an article submitted by Mr. Zhisheng, titled "Also a Jiangbei Person," which I am specially publishing to express the breath of Jiangbei people. - Editor's Note.

Market News

Dr. Ying Yongfeng, Dentist, is conducting business as usual. Dr. Ying Yongfeng, dentist, is located at No. 9 Ningbo Road, opposite the Shanghai Bank. He returned to his hometown when the Sino-Japanese war broke out, but has now returned to Shanghai and is conducting business as usual.

Lihe Auction House. Lihe Auction House, located at No. 9 Ningbo Road, is famous at home and abroad. It has improved bad habits and treats all entrusted items equally, regardless of the quantity. If people from all walks of life urgently want to turn old furniture and other items into cash, the auction house will provide accurate estimates and give cash immediately, ensuring convenience for both buyers and sellers.

China's Famous Martial Arts Expert Comes to Shanghai. Zhang Baoqing, China's famous martial arts expert, came to Shanghai seven years ago to organize the National Development Technical Troupe. He once performed various amazing martial arts skills and was famous for a time. He then went to North China, Pingjin and other places to perform, and was also warmly welcomed by people in those places. At that time, dignitaries in the north and south presented him with more than 250 medals and plaques. After that, Zhang went to various European countries, such as Germany, Austria, Italy, France, and the Low Countries. Zhang himself said that he went to Russia to study at the age of eight. In his spare time, he liked to practice martial arts. When he grew up, his skills became more refined. After returning to China, he received guidance from famous teachers, and his attainments became even deeper. The most impressive of his skills are the toad dance and the high platform dive. In addition, there are many other amazing skills. His wife, Zhang Cuiying, and more than 20 male and female troupe members all have profound martial arts skills. It is said that Zhang plans to perform in Shanghai in the near future.

High Court First Branch

Criminal First Instance Judgment. Lao Zha Municipal Police Department v. Wang Yaqun, Theft Case (Main Text): Wang Yaqun, repeat offender for theft, sentenced to one year and two months of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the judgment is final shall be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. Lao Zha Municipal Police Department v. Deng Changlin, Theft Case (Main Text): Deng Changlin, repeat offender for theft, sentenced to two years of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the judgment is final shall be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. Hongkou Municipal Police Department v. Wang Genxiang et al., Theft Case (Main Text): Wang Genxiang, guilty of group theft, sentenced to one year of imprisonment. Liu Agen, guilty of group theft, sentenced to six months of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the judgment is final shall be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. The stolen goods shall be claimed by the original owner. General Inspectorate v. Zhang Shenshi, Attempted Sale and Possession of Opium Case (Main Text): Zhang Shenshi, guilty of attempting to sell and possessing opium, sentenced to six months of imprisonment. Guity of attempting to bribe, sentenced to three months of imprisonment. Execute imprisonment for six months. The number of days of detention before the judgment is final shall be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. Probation for three years. Seven small bags of opium and one five-yuan banknote used for bribery are confiscated and the opium is burned. Huishan Municipal Police Department v. Guo Maofa et al., Robbery Case (Main Text): Guo Maofa, guilty of three counts of robbery, sentenced to three years of imprisonment for each count, with deprivation of political rights for three years. The combined sentence is five years of imprisonment, with deprivation of political rights for five years. Guilty of gambling, fined fifty yuan, which will be enforced jointly. If the fine is not paid after compulsory execution, two yuan will be converted into one day of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the judgment is final shall be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. The pistol and bullets are confiscated. The stolen goods are stored in the warehouse for claiming. Cao Shaomo is innocent. The shotgun, pistol, bullets, and silverware are returned. Li Boying et al. v. Jiang Zhonghe et al., Fraud Case (Main Text): This case is not accepted. Zhao Ziguang v. Wang Caikun et al., Injury Case (Main Text): Wang Caikun and Kong Shoushan, jointly guilty of injuring a person, each sentenced to forty days of detention, with two years of probation. Hongkou Municipal Police Department v. Lin Xiang et al., Opium Case (Main Text): Lin Xiang, Liang Jinchu, Chen Zhangshi, and Chen Cheng, guilty of attempting to sell and possessing opium, each sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined one hundred yuan. If the fine is converted into imprisonment, two yuan will be converted into one day. The number of days of detention before the judgment is final shall be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. The opium, opium paraphernalia, and opium funds are confiscated. Yao Tingguang v. Feng Dewei, Defamation Case (Main Text): This case is not accepted. Hongkou Municipal Police Department v. Kussnievich, Obstruction of Official Duty Case (Main Text): Kussnievich, guilty of using violence against a public official performing his duties, sentenced to three months of imprisonment. Guilty of violating police regulations, fined ten yuan. If not paid, one yuan will be converted into one day of detention. Wang Baosheng v. Wu Kaiyuan et al., Suspected Injury Case (Main Text): Wu Kaiyuan and Wu Sunshi are innocent. The incidental civil suit of the plaintiff is dismissed. Dixiwei Road Municipal Police Department v. Li Xiahe et al., Public Danger Case (Main Text): Li Xiahe, Yang Huaifu, and Hu Jiagen, jointly guilty of possessing explosives, each fined fifty yuan. If the fine is not paid after compulsory execution, two yuan will be converted into one day of imprisonment. Two bags of gunpowder are confiscated. Yangshupu Municipal Police Department v. Hu Kaibao, Theft Case (Main Text): Hu Kaibao, guilty of theft, sentenced to one month of detention. General Inspectorate v. Ma You, Stolen Goods Case (Main Text): Ma You, guilty of receiving stolen goods, fined twenty yuan. If not paid, two yuan will be converted into one day of detention. Lao Zha Municipal Police Department v. Qu Ali, Theft Case (Main Text): Qu Ali, guilty of theft, sentenced to one month of detention. General Inspectorate v. Chen Yundun, Embezzlement Case (Main Text): Chen Yundun, guilty of embezzling lost property, fined thirty yuan. If not paid, two yuan will be converted into one day of detention. Dixiwei Municipal Police Department v. Wu Zhengze, Obstruction of Official Duty Case (Main Text): Wu Zhengze, guilty of using violence against a public official performing his duties, sentenced to two months of imprisonment. Hongkou Municipal Police Department v. Chen Maoji, Fraud Case (Main Text): Chen Maoji, guilty of fraud, sentenced to six months of imprisonment. Lao Zha Municipal Police Department v. Chen Yongsheng, Opium Case (Main Text): Chen Yongsheng, guilty of possessing opium, fined fifty yuan. If the fine is not paid, two yuan will be converted into one day of detention. Six and a half ounces of opium are confiscated. Lao Zha Municipal Police Department v. Ding Changming, Theft Case (Main Text): Ding Changming, guilty of theft, sentenced to one year of imprisonment. Hongkou Municipal Police Department v. Song Wushi, Fraud Case (Main Text): Song Wushi, guilty of fraud, sentenced to one month of detention. Jiaxing Municipal Police Department v. Zhu Xiaojing et al., Injury Case (Main Text): Zhu Xiaojing and Zhu Jintang, jointly guilty of injury, each sentenced to fifteen days of detention. Civil First Instance Judgment. Hardy Weilly Love v. Tongronggen, Ordering Case (Main Text): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff the price of goods in the amount of 2,215 taels and 1 mace of silver, as well as interest at an annual rate of 7% from January 13 of this year until the end of the execution, and shall deliver the uncollected goods to the plaintiff. The remaining claims and the application for provisional execution are dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. Civil Instructions. Shanghai Second Special District District Court

▲Civil Judgment: Zhan Peilin vs. Huanan Chemical Industry Co. promissory note case (Main Text): The defendant should repay the plaintiff the sum of one thousand four hundred and forty-two yuan in promissory notes. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. This case should be subject to provisional execution. ▲ Yao Jiayin vs. Fang Xinhou promissory note case (Main Text): The defendant should pay the plaintiff two hundred taels of silver and deferred interest at the rate of six percent per annum from June 20th of the Republic of China until the date of termination of execution. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. ▲ Shen Amao vs. Wang Heting debt case (Main Text): The defendant should compensate the plaintiff two hundred yuan. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. Wang Hanlun vs. Hehe Gongji Jingzu Zhangfang rent arrears appeal (Main Text): The original judgment is reversed, except for the portion where the appellant should settle one hundred and ten taels of secondary rent silver and fifteen yuan to the appellee. The appellee's lawsuit in the first instance is dismissed except for the aforementioned excluded portion. The appellant shall bear three-fifths of the litigation costs in this instance and the first instance, and the appellee shall bear two-fifths. ▲ Lu Binjian vs. Jin Gengyu et al. debt case (Main Text): The defendant Jin Gengyu should repay the plaintiff three thousand yuan and interest at the rate of one cent and six li per month from June 15th of the Republic of China until the date of termination of execution. If the execution is ineffective, the defendant Jin Yingqi shall pay on his behalf. The plaintiff's remaining claims are dismissed. The plaintiff shall bear one-third of the litigation costs, and the remaining portion shall be borne equally by the defendants Jin Gengyu and Jin Yingqi. ▲ Meilin Company vs. Pan Zhenghe arrears case (Main Text): The defendant should repay the plaintiff four thousand seven hundred and sixty-one yuan. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

The petition is noted. This court previously conducted a provisional attachment of the movable property of Kai Ai Fu Ma Le. According to Chinese law, the provisional attachment is a preservation procedure and has not reached the stage of compulsory execution. If the petitioner wishes to participate in the distribution, he can leisurely file a lawsuit in the Civil Court to obtain a judgment for review. The precedents of the former Supreme Court and the interpretations of the Judicial Yuan cited in the letter refer to the time of execution, and the previous provisional attachment is a preservation procedure that has not yet been executed. Furthermore, a clear instruction has been issued to file a lawsuit in the Civil Court, so it should proceed according to law. How can it be said to be a rebuttal? You are to file a lawsuit within ten days. ▲ One case: Ke Huailian and Foji petition for execution. The petition is noted. The debtors Ai Po Ruo Fu, etc., have already declared an appeal. ▲Criminal Judgment: Ruling on the case where the prosecutor of this court requested to determine the sentence to be executed for Huang Ahuan for theft and escape (Main Text): Wu Ahuan shall be sentenced to ten months of imprisonment. The number of days of detention shall still be calculated at two days for one day of imprisonment. ▲ Zhou Da Laizi, i.e., Da Gangzi, case of intimidation (Main Text): Zhou Da Laizi, i.e., Zhou Da Gangzi, jointly intended to illegally possess property and used intimidation to cause others to deliver their property. Sentenced to thirty days of detention. The number of days of detention shall be calculated at two days for one day of detention. ▲ Luo Kaiming theft case (Main Text): Luo Kaiming took advantage of a disaster to commit attempted theft. Sentenced to six months of imprisonment. The number of days of detention shall be calculated at two days for one day of imprisonment. ▲ Wu Yuefu sues Shen Zhixian for fraud (Main Text): This private prosecution is not accepted. ▲ Shi Guojie opium case (Main Text): Shi Guojie intended to sell opium and transported it, a crime. Sentenced to two years of imprisonment and fined one hundred yuan. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, it shall be converted to detention at a rate of two yuan per day. The number of days of detention shall be calculated at two days for one day of imprisonment. ▲ Xu Mingke et al. robbery and possession of military firearms and ammunition case (Main Text): Xu Mingke, Kong Chuyu, Sun Zizhou, Zhu Keqing, and Hua Zhiben, colluded, three men, carrying weapons, destroyed the door fence and entered to rob at night, a crime. Each sentenced to eight years of imprisonment and deprived of public rights for eight years. The number of days of detention shall be calculated at two days for one day of imprisonment. One six-inch Browning pistol, fourteen bullets, and one magazine are confiscated.
